data-testid="drop-cap-letter" data-el="text" class="wpds-c-cYdRxM wpds-c-cYdRxM-iPJLV-css overrideStyles font-copy" dir="null">For several years, Oman had promised them a new life. The quiet Persian Gulf monarchy had given 28 Yemenis — transferred there from the U.S. military prison at Guantánamo Bay, Cuba — housing, health care and jobs, and even helped them find wives and start families. It was a stunning turn of fortune after years of abusive interrogations and detention without charge.</p></div></div><div></div></div><div class="wpds-c-jkoBlc
